#### Introduction

Every person developing technologies at aixeno inc. and aixeno.com intends to deliver beneficial technologies to everyone, by being fair, reasonable, and consistently lawful in all business relationships and transactions with customers, consumers, and end-users: this legal webpage is the guide for how we intend to deal with everyone fairly and in good faith.

This webpage describes and explains important legal information, rules, agreements, regulations, and policies that altogether apply to; the company aixeno inc. and its technologies, how those technologies are provided to consumers, customers, and end-users through the website  [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "click or tap to go to aixeno.com - https://aixeno.com")  and how to lawfully use those technologies during any business relationships, and transactions with aixeno inc.

  

#### Please Read All Legal Information

Please read carefully all legal notices, details, terms and conditions of lawful use before using any aixeno solutions and creations, including without limitation: any websites, apps, software, or other technologies, other data, and other aixeno information.  
  
**If you do not agree to the legal information, rules, agreements, regulations, policies, and terms of use, on this legal webpage, then you are strictly prohibited from using anything created, owned, controlled or affiliated with aixeno inc.**  
  
By using any aixeno inc. website(s), or web links or email links on this site or affiliate sites, (or by using any apps, software, and technologies, data, or information of aixeno), your use of, and benefit from, any information on this website and affiliated websites, or apps, software, and technologies of aixeno inc., will be interpreted by the company as your unconditional acceptance and agreement to comply in good faith with the terms, conditions, policies and legal requirements listed below.

  

#### Legal Documents Are All Connected And Legally Binding

Legal documents of aixeno inc. and aixeno.com are all connected to each other, affect each other, depend upon each other, and are "integrated together." Legal documents of aixeno inc. and aixeno.com includes (without limitation): legal information, laws, rules, regulations, legal agreements, licenses, contracts, policies, legal notices, legal requirements, terms and conditions, code of conduct, cybersecurity policies, privacy policies, and any laws applying to any transactions and business relationships of aixeno inc. and aixeno.com. All legal documents of aixeno inc. and aixeno.com are legally binding upon customers, consumers, and end-users of aixeno products, services, data, information, websites, app, software, and anything else that is connected to or controlled by aixeno inc. Since customers, consumers, and end-users get to use the digital solutions and digital technologies of aixeno through the company website aixeno.com, then all website terms and conditions apply to the technology license agreement. The privacy policy, cookie policy, legal information, legal notices, all other legal documents, and any legal requirements, then also all apply to the website terms and conditions and the license agreements.

  

#### United States Law on the International Use of Technologies Made in the USA

ai technologies, apps, software, and other products and services of aixeno inc., may not be available to all persons and entities in all countries, as United States of America (“USA”) Export Law may restrict or prohibit their use.  Please see the legal requirements and restrictions:  [Export Policy Restrictions - aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/legal.html#6.%20%20Export%20Policy%20&%20Restrictions "Export Policy Restrictions - aixeno.com/legal.html").

#### 3\. Jurisdiction & Venue

Washington State Law applies to all issues of legal jurisdiction and venue. Your use of anything that the company creates and makes available to public markets or anything that is offered as a technology solution through the website [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "click or tap to go to aixeno.com - https://aixeno.com") includes (but is not limited to): apps, software, data, information, technology, digital services, digital products, websites, web applications delivered by software as a service "web app saas," artificial intelligence "ai," digital data, digital information, networks, technology contracts, technology services, quantum computing software, intellectual property created and owned by the company, and any company property used to provide consumers any digital services or digital products; shall altogether and / or individually, be completely governed by, and its legal meaning be construed in accordance with, the internal substantive laws of the State of Washington, U.S.A., without reference to any conflicts of law provisions. Your use of any of those solutions will be interpreted by this company (aixeno inc.) that you unconditionally agree that any action at law or in equity arising out of or relating to any licenses, transactions, terms, conditions, policies, procedures, actions, exchange of information, regarding any aixeno solutions and technologies, shall only be filed, and that venue properly lies, only in State or Federal Courts located in the State of Washington, County of Spokane, City of Spokane, and, that you hereby consent freely and submit lawfully to the personal jurisdiction of such courts for the purposes of litigating any legal action(s). The company aixeno inc., makes no representation that any solutions, technologies, products, services, information, digital content on any aixeno inc. website, is or will always be appropriate, available, or suitable for any use of any kind or for use in any particular location, anywhere in the world. Those who choose to use any aixeno solutions, technologies, or information, including but not limited to any access any aixeno inc. websites, that they do so, entirely by their own initiative and they are aware that they entirely assume all risks and expenses they create or cause by their access, transaction, and / or use, and that they are entirely and exclusively responsible for their good-faith compliance with all applicable laws imposed upon them from any Federal, State, Local (and / or any International or Country-specific applicable laws).

#### 4\. Company Business Purpose

aixeno is a software publisher creating new artificial intelligence technologies, apps, software, and digital solutions for work.

#### 5\. Company Markets

As a software publisher, aixeno inc. creates, develops and publishes software applications and technologies for business and personal use on mobile devices, web apps, desktop computers, and cloud platforms, for a variety of different technology markets. The company's market emphasis is: first, Business to Consumer ("B2C"), followed by other types of market categories. The company's primary technology platform used to deliver available products and services to the public marketplace of consumers is a web application software as a service ("web app saas") model, commonly known as a 'web app,' available on the internet. The company does not currently offer any apps or software that may be purchased and downloaded to any digital devices. The company does offer digital data and digital information products and services. The types of customers the company serves, includes (without limitation): human persons; and other entities commonly referred to as: businesses; non-profits; governments; non-government organizations; charitable organizations, educational institutions, and scientific organizations. Web app software services are unavailable for the following platforms & services: application programming interfaces - (APIs), webhooks - (WHKs), and machines to machines - (M2Ms). The company's products and services are not available to citizens and entities of specific countries as required by U.S. Law Export Restrictions, and by the company's business choice to avoid specific technology markets that are considered to be high risk for cybersecurity reasons. Please see below the sections titled "Export Policy & Restrictions" and "Technology Market Exclusions."

#### 6\. Export Policy & Restrictions

ai technologies, apps, software, and other products and services of aixeno inc., may not be available to all persons and entities in all countries, as United States of America (“USA”) Export Law may restrict or prohibit their use.

The company aixeno inc., is a USA based company: it offers digital solutions and digital technologies in the form of digital goods, digital services, artificial intelligence "ai" applications ("ai apps"), software, digital data and information, and other ai technologies, through the website [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "click or tap to go to aixeno.com - https://aixeno.com").

USA Law governs all offers made by the company to grant a user license for digital solutions and technologies to customers and are therefore offered on the condition that the person or entity is **not** legally prevented from viewing, accessing, or acquiring a license to use the solutions and technologies, according to USA Export Law.

USA Export Law applies to ai digital solutions and technologies in three situations: (1) you the consumer are living in, under the control of, or a national or resident of; Russia, Belarus, People's Republic of China, Cuba, Iran, North Korea, Sudan, Syria, or Myanmar, (or a national or resident of one of these countries); or, (2) you are on the USA Treasury Department's Specially Designated Nationals List or the U.S. Commerce Department's Denied Persons List, Unverified List or Entity List; or, (3) you intend to supply the acquired goods, services or software to Russia, Belarus, People's Republic of China, Cuba, Iran, North Korea, Sudan, Syria, or Myanmar, (or a national or resident of one of these countries) or to a person on the Specially Designated Nationals List, Denied Persons List, Unverified List or Entity List.  More detailed information about U.S. Export Law may be found at the United States Bureau of Industry and Security Website:  [U.S. Bureau of Industry & Security - List of Parties of Concern](https://www.bis.doc.gov/index.php/policy-guidance/lists-of-parties-of-concern "U.S. Bureau of Industry & Security - List of Parties of Concern")  Please consult the United States Department of Treasury Office of Foreign Assets Control - Sanctions Programs and Information website:  [United States Department of Treasury Office of Foreign Assets Control - Sanctions Programs and Information](https://home.treasury.gov/policy-issues/office-of-foreign-assets-control-sanctions-programs-and-information "United States Department of Treasury Office of Foreign Assets Control - Sanctions Programs and Information").

Before acquiring a license to use the digital solutions and technologies, every customer must truthfully disclose the following: that by viewing, accessing, or acquiring a license to use any digital products, digital services, digital data and information, or other digital technologies, through any of the aixeno inc. websites, that you the consumer, lawfully disclose and represent information to the company truthfully and accurately, that your viewing, accessing, use and acquisition of a license to use the solutions and technologies listed above, altogether complies with all USA Legal requirements and all USA Export Law Restrictions. Customer's disclosures must be made in all situations, by all types or categories of customers, for any use of the company's digital solutions and technologies, for the intended and actual use anywhere in the world.

Any customer that is a prevented by USA Export Law from using or acquiring digital solutions and technologies, if they are restricted and / or altogether subject to United States export control and economic sanctions requirements, will not be eligible to receive or accept any offers from this company for any digital solutions or digital technologies, and no payments will be accepted from those customers, for anything, under any circumstances or conditions.

The company aixeno inc., when complying in good faith with USA Export Law Restrictions, Sanctions, or other USA Laws, will have **no legal liability or obligation of any kind** to potential customers that have been refused a license, refused acceptance of any fees paid in order to use any of the company's goods and/or services, or otherwise refused access or any use to the company's digital solutions, digital technologies, or digital information, anywhere in the world. In any case where aixeno inc. must not make an offer to a customer, must rescind an offer to a customer, must deny access to a customer, and must deny the issuance of any license to a customer for any use of any digital goods, digital services, digital information, or digital technologies of the company to any customer because of any compliance requirements that aixeno inc. must follow by law, then the company aixeno inc. shall have **no liability, obligation, or duty to pay monetary damages of any kind**, to any customer who is denied access and denied a license to use any technological goods or services of aixeno.com and aixeno inc.

#### 7\. Technology Market Exclusions

As a software publisher, aixeno inc. creates, develops and publishes software applications and technologies for business and personal use as web applications "web apps" and cloud platforms, for a variety of different technology markets.

aixeno inc. does not provide services or goods in the following markets or industries:

(1) aixeno inc. is not a "common carrier" in the U.S.A. or in any other country, as that term is defined in the U.S.A. by statute 47 U.S. Code Part I - Common Carrier Regulation;

(2) aixeno inc. is not a "telecommunications service provider" in the U.S.A. or in any other country, as that term is defined in the U.S.A. by the Telecommunications Act of 1996 and by statutes 47 U.S.C. § 153(50) and 47 U.S.C. § 153(53);

(3) aixeno inc. is not a "mobile communications service provider" in the U.S.A. or in any other country, as those terms are defined in the U.S.A. by statute 47 U.S.C. § 153(33);

(4) aixeno inc. is neither a "social media platform" nor an "internet content provider" in the U.S.A. or in any other country, as those terms are defined in the U.S.A. by statutes 47 U.S.C. § 230(a)(1) (definition of “interactive service.”), and 47 U.S.C. § 706(c)(1).

(5) aixeno inc. is not a platform provider/broker of any virtual currencies or NFTs. aixeno inc. does not offer any goods or services relating to any type of digital assets categorized or defined as any: "virtual currency" and/or "cryptocurrency" and/or "NFTs - (non-fungible tokens)." aixeno inc. does not provide any goods and/or services and/or transactions to anyone engaging in any use of or investment or exchange of virtual currency, cryptocurrency and/or NFTs. aixeno inc. is not a broker/exchange platform for any virtual currency, cryptocurrency, NFTs, and/or any other [digital currency assets](https://www.irs.gov/businesses/small-businesses-self-employed/digital-assets "digital currency assets") in the U.S.A. or in any other country.

(6) aixeno inc., is not a "third-party payment settlement organization - TPSO" in the U.S.A. or in any other country, as that term is defined in the U.S.A. by statute 26 U.S. Code § 6050W. This means that aixeno inc. does not provide any of the following: third-party payments processing, payments sending, payments settlement, payments transmission, payments intermediation, or any services related to those transactions, anywhere in the world (neither in the U.S.A. nor in any other country). aixeno inc. is not a payments settlement entity. aixeno inc. does not provide any third-party financial network platform(s).

(7) aixeno inc., is not an "investment adviser - I.A./R.I.A." in the U.S.A., or in any other country, as that term is defined in the U.S.A. by statute 15 U.S. Code § 80b–2, the U.S. Investment Advisers Act of 1940 Section 202(a)(11), and U.S. State Laws regulating Investment Advisers. This means that aixeno inc. does not provide any advice to others or issue reports or analyses regarding investment securities.

#### 8\. Descriptions of products, services, websites, apps, software, data, information, and other technologies

Solutions - the word "solutions" and the phrase "digital solutions," both refer to all of the digital products and services created by aixeno inc. and made available to consumers through the website aixeno.com.  Solutions include (without limitation) the following descriptions:

ai - artificial intelligence apps - any applications using any type of artificial intelligence technologies.

Web Apps SAAS - web applications delivered by software as a service.

Websites of The Company - websites owned and/or controlled by aixeno inc. are listed below:

* [aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "https://aixeno.com")
* [aixeno.net](https://aixeno.net/ "https://aixeno.net")
* [aixeno.org](https://aixeno.org/ "https://aixeno.org")
* [aixeno.io](https://aixeno.io/ "https://aixeno.io")
* [aixeno.ai](https://aixeno.ai/ "aixeno.ai")
* [aixeno.app](https://aixeno.app/ "https://aixeno.app")
* [aixeno.cloud](https://aixeno.cloud/ "https://aixeno.cloud")
* [aixeno.co](https://aixeno.co/ "https://aixeno.co")
* [aixeno.dev](https://aixeno.dev/ "https://aixeno.dev")
* [aixeno.software](https://aixeno.software/ "https://aixeno.software")
* [aixeno.systems](https://aixeno.systems/ "https://aixeno.systems")
* [aixeno.tech](https://aixeno.tech/ "https://aixeno.tech")
* [aixeno.technology](https://aixeno.technology/ "https://aixeno.technology")

Apps - "apps" means software applications used by a consumer, customer, and/or end-user.

Software - "software" means any electronic digital program instructions (written in any programming language) that gives algorithmic instructions to any website, web application, computer or digital device, altogether used to interact with or to run any operating systems, applications, artificial intelligence, websites, web applications, or is a set of program instructions used to run calculations, instructions and transactions on any computer or digital device.

Digital Services - services used by consumers through any website, web application, computer or other digital device, which are based upon any digital software applications that allow a consumer to get digital information, perform information processing, perform transactions, create or store information, or perform some activity through websites, web applications, computers or digital devices.

Digital Data Products - any digital data and / or information that is made available to consumers for use, sale, subscription, downloading, storing, accessing, processing, updating, or any other use of digital data as a product usable by consumers on their computers or digital devices.

Digital Information Products - any digital data and / or information that is made available to consumers for use, sale, subscription, downloading, storing, accessing, processing, updating, or any other use of digital data as a product usable by consumers on their computers or digital devices.

AI - artificial intelligence "ai" - any technology that is a combination of software and hardware used on any computer machines or digital device machines to process data and information in an intelligent and seemingly autonomous way in real-time, and that accomplishes some computer processing of data, information, transactions, analysis, or suggesting conclusions, that humans would customarily perform.

QCS - quantum computing software - any software used with any quantum computer, such as an operating system, application, other digital solutions used with or to interact with a quantum computer, and other additional software related digital technologies created and used in any way that involves any quantum computer hardware, software or data.

Other Technologies - any other digital solutions and / or digital technologies not already defined above.

#### 9\. Technology Changes, Updates, Publishing and Distribution

The company aixeno inc. makes changes, improvements, and updates to everything it creates (digital solutions and digital technologies) on an ongoing and continuous basis. One, or several updated versions of any or all of each of the digital solutions and digital technologies created by aixeno inc., may be published and distributed to the general public for licensed use during the normal course of business during any calendar year. The company reserves the exclusive right at any time to change any and/or all website(s), webpages, forms, and all other web related features and functions, at its own discretion and without any prior notice to any consumers. The company is not required to seek any prior consent from consumers and end-users before making any changes to any digital solutions or digital technologies, content, features, functions, availability, or any other thing, related to any technology created and controlled by this company. The company aixeno inc., expressly disclaims any obligation or responsibility to any end-users, customers, and consumers, for any of the company's lawful choices made and actions taken to create, change, amend, modify, update, delete or otherwise remove from public use, any part of the company's websites, webpages, forms , features, functions or other digital properties, intellectual properties, web apps, apps, software, and other technologies, from active use, subscription use, and/or licensed use or sale of digital products in commerce and trade anywhere in the world. At any time, the company aixeno inc. may amend, change, update, edit, any or all of its websites(s) and webpages, (including by modification, deletion and/or addition of any portions of anything that the company owns and controls), without prior notice. The company has the exclusive right to publish and distribute anywhere in the world, through any digital platform or device or website, any versions of any digital solutions and digital information made or controlled by the company, including (without limitation): products, services, websites, apps, software, data, information, and other technologies. The company aixeno inc. has the exclusive right to cancel at any time for any reason or for no reason and may decide to stop offering for use or subscription, any web application services, apps, websites, software and any other technologies created by aixeno inc. that are offered for use as a service through the website aixeno.com. The company will provide timely and accurate advance notice of cancelation of any web app software services to all existing customers, with a minimum of thirty ("30") calendar days advance notice before any web application software service is terminated and removed from electronic commerce on the website [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "https://aixeno.com").  The company aixeno inc. may at any time change, edit, amend or remove entirely, any conditions and terms of its licenses to use its digital solutions and technologies.

#### 10\. Artificial Intelligence - Use, Disclosures, Disclaimers

Any use of artificial intelligence, of any kind, by aixeno inc. through the website aixeno.com and use of ai in any of the apps, software, or technologies of aixeno inc. and aixeno.com, will be disclosed on this webpage.

**ai from other vendors - a brief list** aixeno.com may use some or all of the products and services from the following list of ai vendors:  [ai list - ai from other vendors](https://aixeno.com/ailist.html "ai list - ai from other vendors").

**Large Language Models** - OpenAI - the ChatGPT series of technologies are used by several publicly available internet and software technologies that a consumer may encounter when using the internet and a wide variety of apps. [openai.com](https://openai.com/ "OpenAI").

**Microsoft** - any use of Microsoft products and services will often expose the consumer to online interaction with Microsoft's several artificial intelligence driven services, software, and assistants please see: [Microsoft Copilot](https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-copilot "Microsoft Copilot") including use of Large Language Model based ChatGPT in any versions of Copilot, where the GPT model may be driven from OpenAI connected prompts and responses. For more information please see the Microsoft weblinks: [ai intelligent apps](https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/ai/intelligent-apps "https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/ai/intelligent-apps")  [Microsoft Azure Copilot Studio](https://azure.microsoft.com/en-us/products/ai-studio?OCID=copilotbuildc "Microsoft Azure Copilot Studio")  [Microsoft Copilot](https://www.microsoft.com/en-us/microsoft-copilot "Microsoft Copilot").

#### 12\. License to use products, services, websites, apps, software, data, information, and other technologies

**Summary** - a technology license is a temporary permission to use technology: it is not a transfer of or ownership of property. All company licenses granted for technology products and services are temporary and conditioned upon lawful use and good-faith compliance with the terms and conditions of the technology license. End-users, customers, and consumers must pay for their use of and benefit from any products and services from the company, (unless it is free).

aixeno inc. creates solutions: digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, and other technologies, and protects its property rights over those creations by patents, copyrights, trademarks, and other intellectual property right protections. Those solutions are available to end-users through License Agreements. A license agreement is not a transfer of the 'ownership' of the property: it only allows lawful use of the property. License Agreements are necessary legal agreements governing contractual rights and responsibilities of allowable use of all digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, and other technologies created by aixeno inc. A license to use intellectual property owned by the company, aixeno inc., is offered to customers through a License Agreement and customers shall pay a fee (money) to the company for the licensed use. A license to use company intellectual property (goods and/or services) will never grant any ownership rights to any customer(s). License agreements contain contractual terms and conditions that vary, to cover the legal details of different factors, including (without limitation): technology, data, price, access to and delivery of product or service, contract rights, restrictions, service levels, duration of use, and several other considerations. License agreements allow an end-user to enjoy temporary use of digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, and other technologies, created and published by aixeno inc. Licensed use of intellectual properties owned by this company includes (without limitation): apps, software, and other technologies created by aixeno inc., that are offered to customers for licensed use of company created technological services or products. In all cases, the company, aixeno inc., retains all ownership rights over its intellectual property. All digital solutions and digital technologies of aixeno inc. are available to consumers to use through authorized use of a revocable license granted by the company. Consumers do not get any property rights or ownership rights in any digital solutions and digital technologies of the company. All licenses available to consumers of company digital solutions and digital technologies: (a) are not exclusive to any one consumer, person or entity; (b) are not transferable to any other consumer, person or entity under any circumstances; (c) cannot be partially or totally sublicensed; (d) cannot be exported or re-exported; (e) are revocable; (f) are limited by time; and (g) are limited by a conditional right to access and use the digital solutions and digital technologies of this company aixeno inc. through the website aixeno.com only for lawful purposes and lawful uses.

The company aixeno inc., acting through the website aixeno.com, allows consumers to use its digital solutions and digital technologies through a license. Each license contains legal terms and conditions. Generally, license agreements vary, to cover different factors, including (without limitation): technology, data, price, access to and delivery of product or service, contract rights, restrictions, service levels, duration of use, and several other considerations.

Technology - the application of scientific knowledge to research, create, develop, manufacture, and use for primarily practical purposes, any tools, machines, applications, computers, digital electronics, information, data, altogether to accomplish some type of action, work, communication, calculation, processing, transaction, or other activity in the real world. Digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, other technologies, and any additional products, goods, or services, described as "the technological thing being used" in a license agreement and/or service agreement.

Data - electronic data, created and/or provided by aixeno inc. to end-users through a license agreement.

Price - the amount of money or other valuable consideration asked for or given in exchange for something else; it is what is paid for something bought or sold. It is also the amount of money in U.S. Dollars that end-users, consumers, and customers, pay to the company aixeno inc., through a license agreement or service agreement, to use the digital electronic products, services, and data, created by aixeno inc.

Access To & Delivery of Product or Service - descriptions, explanations, and technology details of how to get, use, and benefit from, the digital electronic products, services, and data, created by aixeno inc. and provided through a license agreement.

Contract Rights - a license agreement is a contract: it will contain provisions, terms, and conditions, which are legally binding between the end-user and the company, aixeno inc.

Restrictions - a compliance with or confinement of an action that is done only within bounds, limits, and/or laws. A license agreement will contain restrictions on end-users, regarding; usage time(s) and duration of use until license expires, access points to get and use the technology, the lawful manner of acceptable use of the technology, any geographic/country restrictions mandated by U.S. Law, such as export policy restrictions and any other terms and conditions that define and explain the limits of lawful use of the technology. Limits may include prohibiting any assignment, transfer, decompiling source-code, sharing login in access credentials, confidentiality of license terms, and other lawful restrictions.

Service Levels - a contract dealing with specific terms of an electronic service provided to an end-user, which may contain terms and conditions of: service availability, data speed, quality of service, monitoring of normal operations, fault reporting and response/resolution, division of responsibilities between company versus end-user, failover response systems, backup and recovery, upgrades, maintenance downtime schedules, cybersecurity risk management, security audit procedures and schedules, and several other terms and conditions.

Duration Of Use - the "lifetime of the license" defined in a license agreement: a limited timeline of when the license agreement begins and ends (e.g., (1). a 'monthly recurring subscription license' would be good and valid for one calendar month, (2). an 'annual license' would be in existence and valid for one year (365 days), while (3). a 'perpetual license' would be valid forever).

Term & Termination - similar to the "lifetime of the license" the "Term & Termination" clause of a license agreement describes and explains how long in time the license exists ("Term"), and how the license can be ended ("Termination"), such as the expiration of the life of the license (a one year license expires and becomes invalid and un-usable after 365 days of use), the license can be canceled/terminated by the end-user, or the license can be revoked by the company aixeno inc. according to the terms of the license agreement.

Other Considerations - several additional things expressly listed in a license agreement, including (without limitation): facts, circumstances, intended use, available technology versus applicable technology, commercial reasonableness, impacts upon workplace efficiency, impacts upon society, legal compliance requirements, contract law, intellectual property law, technology development priorities, end-user requests, and many other issues, facts and laws are all relevant to creating a license agreement that is helpful to both end-users and the company.

Property Rights - legal rights (as defined by laws that are existing and apply to any specific type of property) and legal privileges of ownership and control in any tangible or intangible property: legal rights of ownership and enjoyment of use in anything of value that can be identified as property. aixeno inc. retains all ownership property rights (patent, copyright, trademark, and any other intellectual property rights) over everything it creates and publishes for use through license agreements (digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, and other technologies).

Technologies Available for license agreements - some examples of things that may be covered by a license agreement include, (without limitation): digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, and other technologies, created and published by aixeno inc.

end-user - an "end-user " includes (without limitation): human persons, businesses, governments and/or departments & agencies of a government, non-governmental entities, charities, non-profits, educational institutions, scientific institutions, libraries, and/or anyone using computer resources of any of those end-users.

License, Revocable License - permission granted to another person by the company to lawfully use something of value created by the company without passing ownership to another person. A "license," as in 'software license,' is a legal term, meaning that a license is a legally binding agreement between the company, aixeno inc., and an end-user, related to the lawful use of the digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, and other technologies, created by aixeno inc. A revocable license is any license that can or may be canceled, withdrawn, reversed, undone, or annulled.

License Types - the types of license agreements aixeno inc. offers are:

Free License - a general license agreement that applies to any market of end-users, governing the use of digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, and other technologies, by many end-users and made available for free to any end-user .

Trial License - a general license agreement that applies to a specifically limited number of days of free use (e.g., 14 days) to allow a potential end-user to "try before you buy." This license agreement may be issued to any market of end-users, governing the use of digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, and other technologies, by many end-users and made available for free during a limited time to any public market.

Paid License - a general license agreement that applies to any market of end-users, governing the use of digital electronic products, services, data, apps, software, and other technologies, by many customers in a public market and made available for paid use - ( end-users pay money to the company aixeno inc., to use the licensed technology ).

Custom License - a unique license agreement and/or service agreement that involves the creation of or requires any combination of: (a). custom-made digital electronic products, services, and data; (b). a unique combination of contract services, service level agreements, and existing technologies created by aixeno inc.; (c). long-term agreements governing digital electronic products, services, and data; (d). requests to create any type of brand-new technologies involving aixeno inc. digital electronic products, services, and data; (e). any other license agreement for any end-user that is not already defined by the "license types" already listed above.

Since our full-time efforts and resources are spent on developing our own work/projects/research, and since aixeno inc. is a private company, it is the company policy of aixeno inc. that the company is not allowed in any case or in any situation, to accept or consider Unsolicited Submissions. The company wants to avoid the possibility of any frivolous legal actions and misunderstandings when projects developed by us or under our direction might seem to others to mistakenly be similar to other creative work. By using any part of the company owned or controlled websites of aixeno inc., you unconditionally and forever agree that (a) you will not make any Unsolicited Materials/Submissions/Proposals to the company or to anyone associated with the company aixeno inc., and (b) that you cannot create unilaterally any implied contract with the company aixeno inc. and that without our prior express written consent you will never be made to hold any of the company's proprietary or creative information in confidence or trust with the company aixeno inc. and further that there will never be any confidential or fiduciary relationship that should be implied/inferred/or intended to be created, between you and the company aixeno inc. in any way, and that you have no expectation of any access to, review of, or compensation or consideration for anything of any type, at any time.

##### Health Risk Warning & Disclaimer – Photosensitivity – Risk Of Possible Seizures

Any customer that has been diagnosed by a lawfully licensed Physician as having any type of epilepsy or seizures should not use any websites, webpages, videos, media, pictures, images, apps, software, technologies, goods, and services, that are created and/or published by aixeno inc. ##### Customer Data - Information Collection And Use

Website - when a website/webpage of aixeno.com is viewed, aixeno inc. collects viewers' internet data for each viewing session. The website viewing information is collected electronically and securely through internet session security monitoring software and third-party security vendors: it is used by the company aixeno inc. through the website aixeno.com to confidentially and internally, to administer, update and protect all necessary and safe web site security features of the website(s) and webpage(s): the prime use of that data is for the purpose of website security. Website viewing information and public data capture for each website viewing session, may include (without limitation); viewers origin IP address, the webpage viewed and time viewed, viewer's internet browser user agent(s), country of originating internet traffic for viewing session, the viewer's ASNs - ( autonomous system numbers ), viewer's network pathway / routing information, viewer's internet provider name, viewer's internet browsing session "cookies," and several other publicly available information data points of that viewer's browsing session. For any viewing session on aixeno websites, the electronic data may be used altogether as a dataset to be analyzed for website security purposes. This process of using viewer session data is considered worldwide in the technology industry as a standard practice in commerce that is commonly used by most internet service providers and cybersecurity vendors. Internet "cookies" are pieces of electronic data stored in a temporary file that a web site sends to a user's computer while the user is viewing the site. Cookies identify a viewer's web browser, and it is a file that contains and stores information about viewer's website visits, but they generally do not reveal any personally identifiable information. Cookies are used to understand what parts of a website users/viewers are visiting, so as to help identify viewing patterns to improve both security and usability of a website. Contact Form(s) - to communicate with aixeno.com and aixeno inc., anyone using the website [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "https://aixeno.com") may use the link titled "contact" to voluntarily send a secure message to aixeno.com. Only basic information is requested from the person using the form, such as name, email, phone number, and their message. That information may be given only on a voluntary basis by free choice of the person using the website: it is not required in order to view the website. The information is sent by a secure encrypted form to aixeno.com, for purposes of general communication with the company. Please also see the section titled "Consent to Receive Electronic Communications from Company" on this webpage. Third Parties - products and/or services that may be offered for sale or other use by aixeno inc. and aixeno.com, such as weblinks to non-affiliated third-party Websites, which on their own may offer products or services for sale: aixeno.com and aixeno inc. do not accept payments for, process orders of, or ship merchandise on behalf of, any other third-party vendor. Please be aware that aixeno.com and aixeno inc. do not have any control whatsoever, over any third-parties, and aixeno inc. and aixeno.com does not direct, dictate, or supervise, any of the information collection and use policies of any third-party vendors/entities/business or other unrelated and unaffiliated persons or parties. Please be aware that the company is not responsible for the privacy practices of any other web site(s) outside of the website:  [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "https://aixeno.com").  This company encourages all users of aixeno.com websites, to also carefully read the privacy statements of each web site that they visit for more information on how their own internet browsing information may be collected and used. Information Sharing - the company aixeno inc. does not share information of users of its website(s), unless specifically ordered to do so by a legal authority that has served upon aixeno.com and aixeno inc., a valid court order that would lawfully compel compliance with court-ordered disclosure of user/viewer information, OR if the company is legally obligated to comply with a valid search warrant or subpoena and then must disclose user/viewer information.

  

##### Customer Data Privacy & Protection Regulations - CCPA - GDPR

In the United States, some States have their own customer data privacy laws: one example among many States, is California:  [CCPA](https://oag.ca.gov/privacy/ccpa#:~:text=As%20of%20January%201%2C%202023,personal%20information%20collected%20about%20them. "CCPA - California Consumer Protection Act").  The European Union has specific data privacy laws:  [GDPR](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/PDF/?uri=CELEX:32016R0679 "GDPR - full text of law - EU").  Other U.S. States and Other Countries, have their own customer data privacy laws, which contain laws, regulations, and rules, which are altogether different from the CCPA and the GDPR.

  

##### Cookies Policy

Washington State Law, (2). the Electronic Transactions Act - (UETA), and (3). the Electronic Signatures In Global & National Commerce - (ESIGN) requirements.

  

##### Consent To Receive Electronic Communications From Company

To communicate with customers, vendors, and other persons or parties, aixeno.com and aixeno inc. send electronic communications during its lawful business activities, for the purposes of delivering: legal disclosures, timely notices, billing and payment communications, product information, updates, price information, and any other lawful information. As may be required by applicable U.S. Federal and State laws, the company, aixeno inc., is required in some situations to first gain prior express written (electronic) consent, before communicating with customers, vendors, and other persons or parties. All communications in electronic form from aixeno.com and aixeno inc., shall be governed by the laws of Washington State and the Uniform Electronic Transactions Act (UETA) and the ESIGN requirements. The company may use different forms of electronic communications and transactions with customers, including (but not limited to): email, printed mail, printed documents, telephone calls, cell phone calls, text messages in SMS format or MMS format, websites, webpages, and/or direct electronic communications on-screen while using company created apps, software, and technology. Consent to receive electronic communications from this company is voluntary. Consent may be given, amended, stopped, withheld, or otherwise changed, at any time, for any reason or for no reason by either the company or the customer, vendor, or any other persons or parties involved in the electronic communication. The basic information required for electronic communication with this company shall be an email address, or a phone number, or a mailing address, and a legally valid name (person’s name, business name, or other entity name). The company has the right to use publicly available information to verify the identity of each person, business, or other entity. Customers buying apps, software, and technology or technologies from this company, shall have the opportunity to give their consent to receive electronic communications from this company during the EULA-end-user license agreement, at the time of purchase, or through this secure online form. Customers receiving electronic communications from aixeno.com and aixeno inc., shall bear 100% of their own communications costs for their freely chosen vendors that are not related to or affiliated with aixeno.com and aixeno inc., meaning that customers pay 100% of their costs for their vendors of choice that provide electronic media and communication platforms of email, internet connections and transmissions, cell-phone services, telephone services, or any other electronic communications providers fees of any kind. Customers pay 100% of their own data, message, and usage fees in all cases. Electronic signatures used for consent to receive communications from aixeno.com and aixeno inc., shall be governed by the laws of Washington State and the Uniform Electronic Transactions Act (UETA) and the ESIGN requirements. The consent form shall use the following text: "Electronic Signature - I give my express written consent by electronic signature on this consent form, for the sole purpose of proving my intent to receive communications from aixeno.com and aixeno inc. If I am giving my electronic signature on behalf of a business or other entity, I represent to aixeno.com and aixeno inc. that I am an “authorized signer” acting with prior authorization on the behalf of the business or other entity I represent. By giving my electronic signature, I agree that I am able to view, read, understand, and accept the “consent to receive electronic communications” information in this document, and further that I give my consent voluntarily and freely. I understand that my consent may be started, stopped, changed and/or revoked at any time, for any reason or for no reason, by either myself, and/or the company/entity that I represent. I understand that the company aixeno.com and aixeno inc., retains their rights at all times to change/update their business communications that may be sent to me, and that any changes in those communications may be made at any time, for any reason or for no reason. If I send any “notice of termination of consent” to stop my existing consent to receive electronic communications from aixeno.com and aixeno inc., that termination notice will be in writing (electronic or printed format) and will be delivered promptly to the company aixeno.com and aixeno inc. either electronically or through the mail delivery system(s) of the U.S.A. to the official company mailing address. Finally, my electronic signature applies only to electronic communications with aixeno.com and aixeno inc. and does not create any implied contract that would involuntarily obligate aixeno.com and aixeno inc.” Customers buying apps, software, and technology or technologies from this company, shall have the opportunity to give their consent to receive electronic communications from this company during the EULA-end-user license agreement, at the time of purchase, or through a secure online form and weblinks:

[consent to receive electronic communications from aixeno.com and aixeno inc](https://www.jotform.com/sign/230555236515049/invite/01gt4zdvv321340e9ddb436cf0 "consent to receive electronic communications from aixeno.com and aixeno inc.").

##### Unsolicited Materials, Submissions, Proposals, Are Not Accepted

aixeno inc. defines the words and phrases "Materials, Submissions, Proposals" to mean text, messages, ideas, concepts, pitches, suggestions, stories, screenplays, treatments, formats, artwork, photographs, drawings, videos, audiovisual works, musical compositions (including lyrics), sound recordings, characterizations, software code, your and/or other persons' names, likenesses, voices, usernames, profiles, actions, appearances, performances and/or other biographical information or material, funding inquiries, internship inquiries, employment inquiries, and/or any other similar materials that you submit, post, upload, embed, display, communicate or otherwise distribute (collectively, "Distribute") on or through an aixeno inc. website by email or by any other means or method. "Unsolicited" means anything that is submitted to aixeno inc. by any means or method, where: (a) the company aixeno inc. did not expressly request or ask you to provide to us via any feature or activity or email on an aixeno inc. website, through any form of electronic communication, or otherwise; and/or (b) on your own accord and without our knowledge and without prior express written consent of the company aixeno inc., that you distribute, send, email, or mail to the company aixeno inc. through any form of electronic communication, or other means or method of delivery. Since our full-time efforts and resources are spent on developing our own work/projects/research, and since aixeno inc. is a private company, it is the company policy of aixeno inc. that the company is not allowed in any case or in any situation, to accept or consider Unsolicited Submissions. Do not mail, email, send or otherwise distribute Unsolicited Submissions on or through any aixeno inc. websites. The company wants to avoid the possibility of any frivolous legal actions and misunderstandings when projects developed by us or under our direction might seem to others to mistakenly be similar to other creative work. By using any part of the company owned or controlled websites of aixeno inc., you unconditionally and forever agree that (a) you will not make any Unsolicited Materials/Submissions/Proposals to the company or to anyone associated with the company aixeno inc., and (b) that you cannot create unilaterally any implied contract with the company aixeno inc. and that without our prior express written consent you will never be made to hold any of the company's proprietary or creative information in confidence or trust with the company aixeno inc. and further that there will never be any confidential or fiduciary relationship that should be implied/inferred/or intended to be created, between you and the company aixeno inc. in any way, and that you have no expectation of any access to, review of, or compensation or consideration for anything of any type, at any time.

#### 26\. Payment Acceptance - Country Restrictions by U.S. Law

Any customer that is a prevented by U.S. Export Law from using or acquiring digital solutions and technologies, if they are restricted and / or altogether subject to United States export control and economic sanctions requirements, will not be eligible to receive or accept any offers from this company for any digital solutions or digital technologies, and no payments will be accepted from those customers, for anything, under any circumstances or conditions. The company aixeno inc., when complying in good faith with U.S. Export Law Restrictions, Sanctions, or other U.S. Laws, will have no legal liability or obligation of any kind to potential customers that have been refused a license, refused acceptance of any fees paid in order to use any of the company's goods and/or services, or otherwise refused access or any use to the company's digital solutions, digital technologies, or digital information, anywhere in the world. In any case where aixeno inc. must not make an offer to a customer, must rescind an offer to a customer, must deny access to a customer, and must deny the issuance of any license to a customer for any use of any digital goods, digital services, digital information, or digital technologies of the company to any customer because of any compliance requirements that aixeno inc. must follow by law, then the company aixeno inc. shall have no liability, obligation, or duty to pay monetary damages of any kind, to any customer who is denied access and denied a license to use any technological goods or services of aixeno inc.

Digital solutions and technologies of aixeno inc. may not be offered to all persons and entities in all countries, as required by U.S. Export Law.

The company aixeno inc., is a U.S. based company: it offers digital solutions and digital technologies in the form of digital goods, digital services, applications ("apps"), software, digital data and information, and other technologies, through the website [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "click or tap to go to aixeno.com - https://aixeno.com").

The company's offers of digital solutions and technologies to consumers are made according to U.S. Law and are therefore offered to customers on the condition that the person or entity is not legally prevented from viewing, accessing, or acquiring a license to use the solutions and technologies, according to U.S. Export Law.

In general terms, U.S. Export Law applies to digital solutions and technologies in three situations: (1) you the consumer are living in, under the control of, or a national or resident of; Russia, Belarus, People's Republic of China, Cuba, Iran, North Korea, Sudan, Syria, or Myanmar, (or a national or resident of one of these countries); or, (2) you are on the U.S. Treasury Department's Specially Designated Nationals List or the U.S. Commerce Department's Denied Persons List, Unverified List or Entity List; or, (3) you intend to supply the acquired goods, services or software to Russia, Belarus, People's Republic of China, Cuba, Iran, North Korea, Sudan, Syria, or Myanmar, (or a national or resident of one of these countries) or to a person on the Specially Designated Nationals List, Denied Persons List, Unverified List or Entity List.  More detailed information about U.S. Export Law may be found at the United States Bureau of Industry and Security Website:  [U.S. Bureau of Industry & Security - List of Parties of Concern](https://www.bis.doc.gov/index.php/policy-guidance/lists-of-parties-of-concern "U.S. Bureau of Industry & Security - List of Parties of Concern")  Please consult the United States Department of Treasury Office of Foreign Assets Control - Sanctions Programs and Information website:  [United States Department of Treasury Office of Foreign Assets Control - Sanctions Programs and Information](https://home.treasury.gov/policy-issues/office-of-foreign-assets-control-sanctions-programs-and-information "United States Department of Treasury Office of Foreign Assets Control - Sanctions Programs and Information").

Before acquiring a license to use the digital solutions and technologies, every customer must truthfully disclose the following: that by viewing, accessing, or acquiring a license to use any digital products, digital services, digital data and information, or other digital technologies, through any of the aixeno inc. websites, that you the consumer, lawfully disclose and represent information to the company truthfully and accurately, that your viewing, accessing, use and acquisition of a license to use the solutions and technologies listed above, altogether complies with all U.S. Legal requirements and all U.S. Export Law Restrictions. Customer's disclosures must be made in all situations, by all types or categories of customers, for any use of the company's digital solutions and technologies, for the intended and actual use anywhere in the world.

#### 27\. Cancelation And Pro-Ration Policy

Consumers and end-users may cancel their subscription to any digital solution or digital technology of aixeno inc. and aixeno.com, for any reason or for no reason, at any time.

Consumers and end-users must request cancelation of any and all subscriptions in writing, or through an email, and/or through the official company contact forms.

The company has the legal right to use commercially reasonable efforts to verify that any cancelation request is from a valid consumer and end-user account, for an existing active subscription, and further the company will verify that the cancelation request is made lawfully by an authorized person, or by an authorized agent of an entity.

The Company will only approve one (1) cancelation request for each one (1) valid and active subscription to any digital solutions and digital technologies of aixeno.com.

If a customer's and end-user's identity, account, and subscription are verified, and if the cancelation request is lawful, then the company will use commercially reasonable efforts to calculate and pro rate any payments received and will evaluate whether any money received by the company as payment(s) for subscription(s) must be refunded and returned to the customer and end-user, according to applicable law.

Pro-Ration applies only to the monthly fixed dollar amount of any subscription cost, price, and fee. Pro-ration does not apply to usage prices, usage costs, variable costs, or variable quantities of data transferred, taxes, fees, surcharges, and/or government required fees, costs, tariffs, duties, and other legally required costs and prices that cannot be pro-rated by applicable law.

Notice of Changes to Cancelation And Pro-Ration Policy - the company aixeno inc., acting through its website aixeno.com, may make any changes to its Cancelation And Pro-Ration Policy at any time, at its sole discretion. At any time, the company aixeno inc. may amend/change/update/edit any or all of its websites(s) and webpages, (including by modification, deletion and/or addition of any portion thereof), without prior notice. The company aixeno inc. will give notice to all end-users of the most recent policy, by publishing the most recent policy on the website & webpage: [legal webpage - https://aixeno.com/legal.html](https://aixeno.com/legal.html "legal webpage - https://aixeno.com/legal.html").

#### 30\. Dispute Resolution

For all legal disputes, the company, aixeno inc., shall decide on a case-by-case basis how best to resolve any/all disputes; it may choose (without limitation): arbitration, mediation, litigation or other lawful methods of dispute resolution, altogether pursued with a goal of achieving fairness & justice when balancing all interests of customers, the company's business purposes, and contributing positively to society.

Notice of Changes to Dispute Resolution Policy - the company aixeno inc., acting through its website aixeno.com, may make any changes to its Dispute Resolution Policy at any time, at its sole discretion. At any time, the company aixeno inc. may amend/change/update/edit any or all of its websites(s) and webpages, (including by modification, deletion and/or addition of any portion thereof), without prior notice. The company aixeno inc. will give notice to all end-users of the most recent policy, by publishing the most recent policy on the website & webpage: [legal webpage - https://aixeno.com/legal.html](https://aixeno.com/legal.html "legal webpage - https://aixeno.com/legal.html").

#### 31\. Arbitration

Arbitration, an alternative dispute resolution process applying to disputes subject to civil law, may be used at the company's discretion, on a case-by-case basis.

Arbitration clauses in arbitration agreements relating to licensed use of digital solutions and digital technologies are not enforceable where those clauses are prohibited by law: some or all of the clauses of an arbitration agreement may not be enforceable against parties who reside in different geographic locations and reside in different jurisdictions.

All consumers are encouraged to consult with their legal counsel to determine whether the arbitration provisions listed in this section are valid and enforceable for consumers in the jurisdiction where they reside.

Consumers may have other rights and remedies in addition to the arbitration provisions listed below.

The parties to this agreement are (the company aixeno inc. acting through its website aixeno.com and the consumer) are altogether ready, able and willing to attempt to resolve any actual disputes that may arise during the existence of this arbitration agreement as a first step, by dealing with each other directly in good-faith and in a civil and lawful manner. All parties to this arbitration agreement mutually promise to notify in writing all other parties that have signed this arbitration agreement, of any dispute, controversy, claim or significant disagreement, and the parties further expressly agree that the promise and pledge to notify the parties is in effect during the existence of this arbitration agreement.

Should any party to this arbitration agreement have any dispute that is not resolved by dealing directly with each other, then as a second step for dispute resolution, then the parties expressly acknowledge that they are willing to arbitrate their dispute(s) in a manner and by using the method required by the jurisdiction of the consumer’s residence.

If the consumer is a resident of the State of Washington, then the place of arbitration shall be Spokane Washington U.S.A. For consumers who are not residents of the State of Washington, the Venue for legal proceedings shall be determined according to applicable law.

The company aixeno inc. is chartered, legally domiciled, and physically located its main office in the city of Liberty Lake, Spokane County Washington, USA.

For residents of Washington State, and as required by law by Spokane County Superior Court’s formal Arbitration legal process, Spokane County Superior Court requires mandatory arbitration for civil cases claiming monetary damages of $100,000 U.S.D. or less. The Court’s purpose of requiring mandatory arbitration is to provide a speedy and fair resolution of civil cases. The arbitrator panel is made up of lawyers in the community who volunteer to serve as arbitrators for the court.

The parties to this arbitration agreement expressly agree to be bound by the following arbitration provisions:

In circumstances of any breach of contract involving any digital solutions and digital technologies made by the company aixeno inc., the company may use arbitration to settle disputes, according to the following terms and conditions. Any controversy, claim, or allegation of breach of contract, that arises out of, or relates to any lawful contracts made by aixeno inc., that are less than $ 100,000 U.S.D., shall be settled by arbitration administered by the American Arbitration Association in accordance with its Commercial Arbitration Rules and judgment on the award rendered by the arbitrator(s) may be entered in any court having jurisdiction thereof. The arbitrator(s) shall be a currently licensed attorney in good standing with the Washington State Bar Association (www.wsba.org). The place of arbitration shall be Spokane, WA, USA. The arbitration shall be governed by the laws of the State of Washington. In making determinations regarding the scope of exchange of electronic information, the arbitrator(s) and the parties agree to be guided by The Sedona Principles, Third Edition: Best Practices, Recommendations & Principles for Addressing Electronic Document Production. Time is of the essence for any arbitration under this agreement and arbitration hearings shall take place within 90 days of filing and awards rendered within 120 days. Arbitrator(s) shall agree to these limits prior to accepting appointment. The arbitrators will have no authority to award punitive or other damages not measured by the prevailing party's actual damages, except as may be required by statute. The arbitrator(s) shall not award consequential damages in any arbitration initiated under this section. Any award in an arbitration initiated under this clause shall be limited to monetary damages and shall include no injunction or direction to any party other than the direction to pay a monetary amount. Pursuant to the Commercial Arbitration Rules of the American Arbitration Association, the arbitrators will have the authority to allocate the costs of the arbitration process among the parties but will only have the authority to allocate attorneys' fees if a particular law permits them to do so. The award of the arbitrators shall be accompanied by a reasoned opinion. Except as may be required by law, neither a party nor an arbitrator may disclose the existence, content, or results of any arbitration hereunder without the prior written consent of both parties. The parties agree that failure or refusal of a party to pay its required share of the deposits for arbitrator compensation or administrative charges shall constitute a waiver by that party to present evidence or cross-examine witness. In such event, the other party shall be required to present evidence and legal argument as the arbitrator(s) may require for the making of an award. Such waiver shall not allow for a default judgment against the non-paying party in the absence of evidence presented as provided for above. Notwithstanding any language to the contrary in the contract documents, the parties hereby agree: that the Underlying Award may be appealed pursuant to the AAA's Optional Appellate Arbitration Rules ("Appellate Rules"); that the Underlying Award rendered by the arbitrator(s) shall, at a minimum, be a reasoned award; and that the Underlying Award shall not be considered final until after the time for filing the notice of appeal pursuant to the Appellate Rules has expired. Appeals must be initiated within thirty (30) days of receipt of an Underlying Award, as defined by Rule A-3 of the Appellate Rules, by filing a Notice of Appeal with any AAA office. Following the appeal process the decision rendered by the appeal tribunal may be entered in any court having jurisdiction thereof.  
  
More information regarding the mandatory Arbitration requirements of Spokane County Superior Courts is available at their website:  
[Spokane County Superior Court - Arbitration - Mandatory Arbitration](https://www.spokanecounty.org/1361/Arbitration "Spokane County Superior Court - Arbitration - Mandatory Arbitration")

#### 32\. Privacy Policy - Customer Data

This Privacy Policy describes the online data collection of customer data from company owned websites and the limited use of that data by the company aixeno inc., specifically data gathered through viewers visiting and using the website: [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "https://aixeno.com") including a description of the types of online information collected and some of the ways in which the company uses that information for internal business purposes, website security, and communications with customers.

###### Information From Children Under Thirteen

The website [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "aixeno.com") is not targeted specifically to children under the age of 13, and the company does not knowingly collect personally identifiable information from any child under the age of thirteen (13) without gaining prior parental consent.

###### Information Collection And Use Of Customer Data

Website - when any webpages of the website aixeno.com are viewed, aixeno inc. collects viewers' internet data for each viewing session. The website viewing information is collected electronically and securely through internet session security monitoring software and third-party security vendors: it is used by the company aixeno inc. through the website aixeno.com to confidentially and internally, to administer, update and protect all necessary and safe web site security features of the website(s) and webpage(s): the prime use of that data is for the purpose of website security. Website viewing information and public data capture for each website viewing session, may include (without limitation); viewers origin IP address, the webpage viewed and time viewed, viewer's internet browser user agent(s), country of originating internet traffic for viewing session, the viewer's ASNs - ( autonomous system numbers ), viewer's network pathway / routing information, viewer's internet provider name, viewer's internet browsing session "cookies," and several other publicly available information data points of that viewer's browsing session. For any viewing session on aixeno websites, the electronic data may be used altogether as a dataset to be analyzed for website security purposes. This process of using viewer session data is considered worldwide in the technology industry as a standard practice in commerce that is commonly used by most internet service providers and cybersecurity vendors. Internet "cookies" are pieces of electronic data stored in a temporary file that a web site sends to a user's computer while the user is viewing the site. Cookies identify a viewer's web browser, and it is a file that stores information about viewer's website visits, but they generally do not reveal any personally identifiable information. Cookies are used to understand what parts of a website users/viewers are visiting, so as to help identify viewing patterns to improve both security and usability of a website. Contact Form(s) - to communicate with aixeno.com and aixeno inc., anyone using the website [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "aixeno.com")  may use the link titled "contact" to voluntarily send a secure message to aixeno.com. Only basic information is requested from the person using the form, such as name, email, phone number, and their message. That information may be given only on a voluntary basis by free choice of the person using the website: it is not required in order to view the website. The information is sent by a secure encrypted form to aixeno.com, for purposes of general communication with the company. Please also see the section titled "_Consent To Receive Electronic Communications From Company_" on this webpage. Third Parties - products and/or services that may be offered for sale or other use by aixeno inc. and aixeno.com, such as weblinks to non-affiliated Third-Party Websites, which on their own may offer products or services for sale: aixeno.com and aixeno inc. do not accept payment for, process orders of, or ship merchandise on behalf of, any other Third-Party Vendor. Please be aware that aixeno.com and aixeno inc. do not have any control whatsoever, over any Third-Parties, and aixeno inc. and aixeno.com does not direct, dictate, or supervise, any of the information collection and use policies of any Third-Party vendors/entities/business or other unrelated and unaffiliated persons or parties. Please be aware that the company is not responsible for the privacy practices of any other web site(s) outside of the website  [https://aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "aixeno.com")  This company encourages all users of aixeno.com websites, to also carefully read the privacy statements of each web site that they visit for more information on how their own internet browsing information may be collected and used. Information Sharing - the company aixeno inc. does not share information of users of its website(s), unless specifically ordered to do so by a legal authority that has served upon aixeno.com and aixeno inc., a valid court order that would lawfully compel compliance with court-ordered disclosure of user/viewer information, OR if the company is legally obligated to comply with a valid search warrant or subpoena and then must disclose user/viewer information.

###### Customer Data Privacy & Protection Regulations - CCPA - GDPR

In the United States, some States have their own customer data privacy laws, one example among many States, is California:  [CCPA](https://oag.ca.gov/privacy/ccpa#:~:text=As%20of%20January%201%2C%202023,personal%20information%20collected%20about%20them. "CCPA - California Consumer Protection Act")  
The European Union has specific data privacy laws:  [GDPR](https://eur-lex.europa.eu/legal-content/EN/TXT/PDF/?uri=CELEX:32016R0679 "GDPR - full text of law - EU")

This company, aixeno inc., defines the words and phrases "Materials," "Submissions," "Proposals," to mean any text, messages, ideas, concepts, pitches, suggestions, stories, screenplays, treatments, formats, artwork, photographs, drawings, videos, audiovisual works, musical compositions (including lyrics), sound recordings, characterizations, software code, your and/or other persons' names, likenesses, voices, usernames, profiles, actions, appearances, performances and/or other biographical information or material, funding inquiries, internship inquiries, employment inquiries, and/or any other similar materials that you submit, post, upload, embed, display, communicate or otherwise distribute (collectively, "Distribute") on or through an aixeno inc. website by email or by any other means or method. "Unsolicited" means anything that is submitted to aixeno inc. by any means or method, that the company aixeno inc.: (a) did not expressly from you and did not request and did not ask you to provide to us through any feature or activity or email on an aixeno inc. website, standard business communication methods, or through any other form of electronic communication, or otherwise; and/or (b) on your own accord and without our knowledge and without our prior express written consent that you distribute, send, email, or mail to the company aixeno inc. through any form of electronic communication, or other means or method of delivery. Since our full-time efforts and resources are spent on developing our own work/projects/research, and since aixeno inc. is a private company, it is the company policy of aixeno inc. that the company is not allowed in any case or in any situation, to accept or consider Unsolicited Submissions. Do not mail, email, send or otherwise distribute Unsolicited Submissions on or through any aixeno inc. websites. The company want to avoid the possibility of any frivolous legal actions and misunderstandings when projects developed by us or under our direction might seem to others to mistakenly be similar to other creative work. By using any part of the company owned or controlled websites of aixeno inc., you unconditionally and forever agree that (a) you will not make any Unsolicited Materials / Submissions / Proposals to the company or to anyone associated with the company aixeno inc., and (b) that you cannot create unilaterally any implied contract with the company aixeno inc. and that without our prior express written consent you will never be made to hold any of the company's proprietary or creative information in confidence or trust with the company aixeno inc. and further that there will never be any confidential or fiduciary relationship that should be implied, inferred, or intended to be created, between you and the company aixeno inc. in any way, and that you have no expectation of any access to, review of, or compensation or consideration for anything of any type, at any time. Unsolicited materials will never create any implied contract of any kind that would involuntarily bind the company aixeno inc.

#### 36\. DMCA - Digital Millennium Copyright Act

The company aixeno inc., acting through the website [aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/ "aixeno company website - https://aixeno.com") complies with the DMCA - Digital Millennium Copyright Act.

In 1998, Congress passed the Digital Millennium Copyright Act (DMCA), which amended U.S. copyright law to address important parts of the relationship between copyright and the internet. The three main updates were (1) establishing protections for online service providers in certain situations if their users engage in copyright infringement, including by creating the notice-and-takedown system, which allows copyright owners to inform online service providers about infringing material so it can be taken down; (2) encouraging copyright owners to give greater access to their works in digital formats by providing them with legal protections against unauthorized access to their works (for example, hacking passwords or circumventing encryption); and (3) making it unlawful to provide false copyright management information (for example, names of authors and copyright owners, titles of works) or to remove or alter that type of information in certain circumstances. [https://www.copyright.gov/dmca](https://www.copyright.gov/dmca/ "DMCA - https://www.copyright.gov/dmca").

The company designates the Chief Executive Officer (CEO) of aixeno inc., as the agent for all DMCA notices and communications from any copyright owner(s), relating to any information contained on any website(s) owned and/or controlled by aixeno inc. Company contacts information are available at this weblink:

[DMCA notice and takedown request to aixeno inc. and aixeno.com](https://form.jotform.com/231263884091054 "DMCA notice and takedown request to aixeno inc. and aixeno.com")

[contact aixeno.com](https://aixeno.com/contact.html "contact information - aixeno inc.")
